\subsection{Detailed Description}
Represents S\+B\+ML errors and other diagnostics. 

\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Author}
Michael Hucka 

Sarah Keating 
\end{DoxyAuthor}


\subsection{Enumeration Type Documentation}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_b_m_l_error_8h_aec82216b5939329921fd2c6f00c62187}\label{_s_b_m_l_error_8h_aec82216b5939329921fd2c6f00c62187}} 
\index{S\+B\+M\+L\+Error.\+h@{S\+B\+M\+L\+Error.\+h}!S\+B\+M\+L\+Error\+Category\+\_\+t@{S\+B\+M\+L\+Error\+Category\+\_\+t}}
\index{S\+B\+M\+L\+Error\+Category\+\_\+t@{S\+B\+M\+L\+Error\+Category\+\_\+t}!S\+B\+M\+L\+Error.\+h@{S\+B\+M\+L\+Error.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{S\+B\+M\+L\+Error\+Category\+\_\+t}{SBMLErrorCategory\_t}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \hyperlink{_s_b_m_l_error_8h_aec82216b5939329921fd2c6f00c62187}{S\+B\+M\+L\+Error\+Category\+\_\+t}}

Category codes for \hyperlink{class_s_b_m_l_error}{S\+B\+M\+L\+Error} diagnostics.

Note that these are distinct from \hyperlink{class_x_m_l_error}{X\+M\+L\+Error}\textquotesingle{}s category codes. User programs receiving an \hyperlink{class_s_b_m_l_error}{S\+B\+M\+L\+Error} object can use this distinction to check whether the error represents a low-\/level X\+ML problem or an S\+B\+ML problem.

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_b_m_l_error_8h_a64521d2629dd339aea5b194d546c3627}\label{_s_b_m_l_error_8h_a64521d2629dd339aea5b194d546c3627}} 
\index{S\+B\+M\+L\+Error.\+h@{S\+B\+M\+L\+Error.\+h}!S\+B\+M\+L\+Error\+Code\+\_\+t@{S\+B\+M\+L\+Error\+Code\+\_\+t}}
\index{S\+B\+M\+L\+Error\+Code\+\_\+t@{S\+B\+M\+L\+Error\+Code\+\_\+t}!S\+B\+M\+L\+Error.\+h@{S\+B\+M\+L\+Error.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{S\+B\+M\+L\+Error\+Code\+\_\+t}{SBMLErrorCode\_t}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \hyperlink{_s_b_m_l_error_8h_a64521d2629dd339aea5b194d546c3627}{S\+B\+M\+L\+Error\+Code\+\_\+t}}

Codes for all S\+B\+M\+L-\/level errors and warnings from the core specification.

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
Calling programs may wish to check which enumeration a given \hyperlink{class_s_b_m_l_error}{S\+B\+M\+L\+Error} object\textquotesingle{}s error identifier is actually from\+: \begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0000000 to 0009999\+: \hyperlink{_x_m_l_error_8h_a5ff7604587bd93fb60cdecb72acd160c}{X\+M\+L\+Error\+Code\+\_\+t} (a low-\/level X\+ML problem)\end{DoxyItemize}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0010000 to 0099999\+: \hyperlink{_s_b_m_l_error_8h_a64521d2629dd339aea5b194d546c3627}{S\+B\+M\+L\+Error\+Code\+\_\+t} (a problem with the S\+B\+ML core specification) \item 1000000 to 1099999\+: \#\+Comp\+S\+B\+M\+L\+Error\+Code\+\_\+t (a problem with the S\+B\+ML Level~3 Hierarchical Model Composition package specification).\end{DoxyItemize}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 2000000 to 2099999\+: \#\+Fbc\+S\+B\+M\+L\+Error\+Code\+\_\+t (a problem with the S\+B\+ML Level~3 Flux Balance Constraints package specification).\end{DoxyItemize}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 3000000 to 3099999\+: \#\+Qual\+S\+B\+M\+L\+Error\+Code\+\_\+t (a problem with the S\+B\+ML Level~3 Qualitative Models package specification).\end{DoxyItemize}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 6000000 to 6099999\+: \#\+Layout\+S\+B\+M\+L\+Error\+Code\+\_\+t (a problem with the S\+B\+ML Level~3 Layout package specification).\end{DoxyItemize}
Other error code ranges are reserved for other packages. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \hyperlink{_s_b_m_l_error_8h_aa4224962df10d5a97c2d79e883b68a72}{S\+B\+M\+L\+Error\+Severity\+\_\+t}}

Severity codes for \hyperlink{class_s_b_m_l_error}{S\+B\+M\+L\+Error} diagnostics.

The only publicly-\/reported values of this type are the four from \hyperlink{_x_m_l_error_8h_a54cf85ac4f9cf6e597bc2cfcb5a6d0f3}{X\+M\+L\+Error\+Severity\+\_\+t}. All other values are used internally only, with translation of those codes done in S\+B\+M\+L\+Error.\+cpp
